# Task: Write Integration Tests for Navidrome Media Scanner

**Repository:** navidrome/navidrome
**Output:** Write your test file to `/workspace/scanner/scanner_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Navidrome's media scanning pipeline. Navidrome scans a music library directory, extracts metadata from audio files, and persists track/album/artist records to a database.

## Scope

Explore the scanner package (`scanner/`) and its dependencies. Key areas:
- `scanner/scanner.go` — top-level scanner entry point
- `scanner/metadata/` — audio file metadata extraction
- `core/artwork/` — artwork extraction
- Database persistence via the store interfaces

Your integration tests must cover:
- Full scan of a test fixture directory with mock audio files
- Metadata extraction (title, artist, album, year, track number)
- Album and artist record creation
- Incremental scan (re-scan with no changes produces no DB updates)
- File deletion detection (missing file removes DB record)

## Output Format

Write a Go test file at:
```
/workspace/scanner/scanner_integration_test.go
```

Use Go's `testing` package. Each test function must start with `Test`. Use test fixtures (small audio files or mock file system) where needed.

## Quality Bar

- At least 5 test functions
- Cover at least 3 pipeline stages (file discovery, metadata extraction, DB persistence)
- Include at least one negative case (deleted file, corrupt metadata)
- Do not fabricate package names or function signatures — inspect the actual codebase first
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

    21→
    22→type Extractor interface {
    23→	Parse(files ...string) (map[string]ParsedTags, error)
    24→	CustomMappings() ParsedTags
    25→	Version() string
    26→}
    27→
    28→var extractors = map[string]Extractor{}
    29→
    30→func RegisterExtractor(id string, parser Extractor) {
    31→	extractors[id] = parser
    32→}
    33→
    34→func LogExtractors() {
    35→	for id, p := range extractors {
    36→		log.Debug("Registered metadata extractor", "id", id, "version", p.Version())
    37→	}
    38→}
    39→
    40→func Extract(files ...string) (map[string]Tags, error) {
    41→	p, ok := extractors[conf.Server.Scanner.Extractor]
    42→	if !ok {
    43→		log.Warn("Invalid 'Scanner.Extractor' option. Using default", "requested", conf.Server.Scanner.Extractor,
    44→			"validOptions", "ffmpeg,taglib", "default", consts.DefaultScannerExtractor)
    45→		p = extractors[consts.DefaultScannerExtractor]
    46→	}
    47→
    48→	extractedTags, err := p.Parse(files...)
    49→	if err != nil {
    50→		return nil, err
    51→	}
    52→
    53→	result := map[string]Tags{}
    54→	for filePath, tags := range extractedTags {
    55→		fileInfo, err := os.Stat(filePath)
    56→		if err != nil {
    57→			log.Warn("Error stating file. Skipping", "filePath", filePath, err)
    58→			continue
    59→		}

    29→func walkDirTree(ctx context.Context, rootFolder string) (<-chan dirStats, <-chan error) {
    30→	results := make(chan dirStats)
    31→	errC := make(chan error)
    32→	go func() {
    33→		defer close(results)
    34→		defer close(errC)
    35→		err := walkFolder(ctx, rootFolder, rootFolder, results)
    36→		if err != nil {
    37→			log.Error(ctx, "There were errors reading directories from filesystem", "path", rootFolder, err)
    38→			errC <- err
    39→		}
    40→		log.Debug(ctx, "Finished reading directories from filesystem", "path", rootFolder)
    41→	}()
    42→	return results, errC
    43→}
    44→
    45→func walkFolder(ctx context.Context, rootPath string, currentFolder string, results chan<- dirStats) error {
    46→	children, stats, err := loadDir(ctx, currentFolder)
    47→	if err != nil {
    48→		return err
    49→	}
    50→	for _, c := range children {
    51→		err := walkFolder(ctx, rootPath, c, results)
    52→		if err != nil {
    53→			return err
    54→		}
    55→	}
    56→
    57→	dir := filepath.Clean(currentFolder)
    58→	log.Trace(ctx, "Found directory", "dir", dir, "audioCount", stats.AudioFilesCount,
    59→		"images", stats.Ima

    19→// refresher is responsible for rolling up mediafiles attributes into albums attributes,
    20→// and albums attributes into artists attributes. This is done by accumulating all album and artist IDs
    21→// found during scan, and "refreshing" the albums and artists when flush is called.
    22→//
    23→// The actual mappings happen in MediaFiles.ToAlbum() and Albums.ToAlbumArtist()
    24→type refresher struct {
    25→	ds          model.DataStore
    26→	lib         model.Library
    27→	album       map[string]struct{}
    28→	artist      map[string]struct{}
    29→	dirMap      dirMap
    30→	cacheWarmer artwork.CacheWarmer
    31→}

    35→		ds:          ds,
    36→		lib:         lib,
    37→		album:       map[string]struct{}{},
    38→		artist:      map[string]struct{}{},
    39→		dirMap:      dirMap,
    40→		cacheWarmer: cw,
    41→	}
    42→}
    43→
    44→func (r *refresher) accumulate(mf model.MediaFile) {
    45→	if mf.AlbumID != "" {
    46→		r.album[mf.AlbumID] = struct{}{}
    47→	}
    48→	if mf.AlbumArtistID != "" {
    49→		r.artist[mf.AlbumArtistID] = struct{}{}
    50→	}
    51→}

    57→	if err := d.writeDB.Close(); err != nil {

    59→	}
    60→}

    64→	err := d.backupOrRestore(ctx, true, destPath)
    65→	if err != nil {
    66→		return "", err
    67→	}

    69→	return destPath, nil
    70→}

   109→// Dirs returns a deduped list of all directories from the MediaFiles' paths
   110→func (mfs MediaFiles) Dirs() []string {
   111→	var dirs []string
   112→	for _, mf := range mfs {
   113→		dir, _ := filepath.Split(mf.Path)
   114→		dirs = append(dirs, filepath.Clean(dir))
   115→	}
   116→	slices.Sort(dirs)
   117→	return slices.Compact(dirs)
   118→}

    39→	pls, err := s.parsePlaylist(ctx, fname, dir)

    42→		return nil, err
    43→	}

    45→	err = s.updatePlaylist(ctx, pls)
    46→	if err != nil {
    47→		log.Error(ctx, "Error updating playlist", "path", filepath.Join(dir, fname), err)
    48→	}

package scanner

import (
	"context"
	"io"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"
	"testing"
	"time"

	"github.com/google/uuid"
	"github.com/navidrome/navidrome/core"

	"github.com/navidrome/navidrome/model"
	"github.com/navidrome/navidrome/tests"
)

// IntegrationMediaFileRepo extends the mock to support scanner-specific methods
type IntegrationMediaFileRepo struct {
	*tests.MockMediaFileRepo
}

func (m *IntegrationMediaFileRepo) FindPathsRecursively(basePath string) ([]string, error) {
	if m.err {
		return nil, nil
	}
	var paths []string
	for _, mf := range m.data {
		if strings.HasPrefix(mf.Path, basePath) {
			paths = append(paths, mf.Path)
		}
	}
	return paths, nil
}

func (m *IntegrationMediaFileRepo) FindAllByPath(path string) (model.MediaFiles, error) {
	if m.err {
		return nil, nil
	}
	var result model.MediaFiles
	for _, mf := range m.data {
		dir := filepath.Dir(mf.Path)
		if filepath.Clean(dir) == filepath.Clean(path) {
			result = append(result, *mf)
		}
	}
	return result, nil
}

func (m *IntegrationMediaFileRepo) FindByPath(path string) (*model.MediaFile, error) {
	if m.err {
		return nil, nil
	}
	for _, mf := range m.data {
		if mf.Path == path {
			return mf, nil
		}
	}
	return nil, model.ErrNotFound
}

func (m *IntegrationMediaFileRepo) FindByPaths(paths []string) (model.MediaFiles, error) {
	if m.err {
		return nil, nil
	}
	var result model.MediaFiles
	pathMap := make(map[string]bool)
	for _, p := range paths {
		pathMap[p] = true
	}
	for _, mf := range m.data {
		if pathMap[mf.Path] {
			result = append(result, *mf)
		}
	}
	return result, nil
}

	if m.err {
		return 0, nil
	}
	var count int64
